     6→ *   Wave 2: L2 SubComponent entities (manifest seeded + code discovery)
     7→ *   Wave 3: L3 Detail entities (pure code discovery)
     8→ *
     9→ * Each wave produces parent nodes before the next wave spawns child-level agents.
    10→ * Entities a
...[truncated]
```
